margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n</div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-94p8vdct-0Q/T-jQBEKbhcI/AAAAAAAAMqg/8mvBvlLS5Fc/s1600/SDFFG.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-94p8vdct-0Q/T-jQBEKbhcI/AAAAAAAAMqg/8mvBvlLS5Fc/s1600/SDFFG.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 115%; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-language: AR-SA; mso-fareast-font-family: Calibri; mso-fareast-language: EN-US; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-latin;\">Okie from Muskogee is an album by Merle Haggard\nand the Strangers, released in 1969. </span><br />\n<br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 115%; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-language: AR-SA; mso-fareast-font-family: Calibri; mso-fareast-language: EN-US; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-latin;\">The album won the Academy of Country Music\naward for Album of the Year in 1969. Haggard also won Single of the Year for\n\"Okie from Muskogee\" as well as Top Male Vocalist</span><br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">In the 1930s in\nCalifornia, the term Okie was used in contempt, to refer to very poor\nimmigrants from Oklahoma . </span><br />\n<br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">The \"Okie\" migration of the 1930s brought\nin over a million new displaced people; many headed to the farms in\nCalifornia's Central valley . The core group of Okies were descendants of\nScotch Irish .<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">The term \"Okie\"\nwas used to disparage these poor, white, migrant workers and their families.\nThe term became well-known nationwide by John Steinbeck's novel The Grapes of\nWrath.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Will Rogers, a famous\nmovie star with Oklahoma roots remarked jokingly that the Okies moving from\nOklahoma to California increased the average intelligence of both states.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><o:p>&nbsp;\n\n</o:p></span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Written by Haggard and\nRoy Edward Burris (drummer for Haggard's backing band, The Strangers) during\nthe height of the Vietnam War, \"Okie from Muskogee\" grew from the two\ntrading one-liners about small-town life, where conservative values were the\nnorm and outsiders with ideals contrary to those ways were unwelcome. </span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n</div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Here, the\nsinger reflects on how proud he is to hail from Middle America, where its\nresidents were patriotic, and didn't smoke marijuana, take LSD, wear beads and\nsandals, burn draft cards or challenge authority. <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>A self-confessed 'square,' is confused by such\nchanges and with a chuckle comes to the conclusion that he and his ilk have the\nright sort of life for themselves.<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span><o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n</div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">By November 15, it\nreached No. 1 on the Billboard magazine Hot Country Singles chart, where it\nremained for four weeks. 1970The song is played in the background in Platoon. The\nsong is referenced in the movies An Officer and a Gentleman<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n</div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">The Vietnam protests\nwere an inspiration on this song - Haggard was protesting the protesters.\nHaggard was imprisoned several times in his younger days for various crimes. </span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">During a 2010 interview with The Boot, he explained: \"When I was in\nprison, I knew what it was like to have freedom taken away. Freedom is\neverything. </span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">During Vietnam, there\nwere all kinds of protests. These soldiers were giving up their freedom and\nlives to make sure others could stay free. I wrote the song to support those\nsoldiers.\"</span><br />\n<br />\nPresident Nixon wanted Johnny Cash to sing this song in White House and he refused.<br />\n<br />\n<span style=\"color: red; font-size: large;\">Say again-- US soldiers fighting in Vietnam to keep America free?</span><br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-zSCMDVh4v30/T-mRTNw5NCI/AAAAAAAAMuY/2WUE3oOJ3mc/s1600/FGHH.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"314\" src=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-zSCMDVh4v30/T-mRTNw5NCI/AAAAAAAAMuY/2WUE3oOJ3mc/s400/FGHH.jpg\" width=\"400\" /></a></div>\n<br />\nPunch into google search <strong><span style=\"color: blue;\">THE GULF OF TONKIN LIE- VADAKAYIL</span></strong><br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-mmlNSZSZUCA/T-mRwNuJVhI/AAAAAAAAMug/9AV9Q9UrWS4/s1600/DFGJJ.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"299\" src=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-mmlNSZSZUCA/T-mRwNuJVhI/AAAAAAAAMug/9AV9Q9UrWS4/s400/DFGJJ.jpg\" width=\"400\" /></a></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Pope Pius XII, Eugenio\nMaria Giuseppe Giovanni Pacelli (2 March 1876 \u2013 9 October 1958), <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>was directly responsible for the American war\nin Vietnam. He used opium drug trade money power to put a Vatican puppet and\nstaunch Roman Catholic president Ngo Dinh Diem, as president of Vietnam in\n1955. </span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-gaRYo1kr_lU/T_FoPsZEOHI/AAAAAAAANDg/_E8UMRLvqcs/s1600/ehjk.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-gaRYo1kr_lU/T_FoPsZEOHI/AAAAAAAANDg/_E8UMRLvqcs/s1600/ehjk.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">His brief was to persecute the Buddhists and convert them to\nChristianity. font-size: large;\"><strong>EDAKKAL CAVES, PHANTOM ROCK, MEENMUTTY WATERFALLS OF WAYANAD KERALA --&nbsp; CAPT AJIT VADAKAYIL</strong></span><br />\n<br />\nI have invested in two cottages ( with swimming pool ) and a piece of land at Meenangadi, Wayanad, 90 kilometers from Calicut.<br />\n<br />\nThis place is&nbsp;2700 feet above sea level and hence will always be 5 degrees cooler than Calicut.&nbsp;The beauty of nature , the wild flora and fauna cannot be described in words.<br />\n<br />\nHere is the Google Earth map.<br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-ig2A24TWiHA/T-fh-3D4-VI/AAAAAAAAMl8/B2XrU-jQf88/s1600/gs.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"369\" src=\"https://2.bp.blogspot.com/-ig2A24TWiHA/T-fh-3D4-VI/AAAAAAAAMl8/B2XrU-jQf88/s640/gs.jpg\" width=\"640\" /></a></div>\n<br />\nIt is very close&nbsp;to Edakkal caves of 12000 BC, in which Neolithic ( sic!) &nbsp;art can be seen. The cave art shows the wheeled cart,&nbsp;and also an ancient script which looks like ancient Malayalam.<br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/--Vvwy8D4ejg/T-fhU6jMsGI/AAAAAAAAMl0/9cIIuj_Qug4/s1600/imagesCAMKRAUV.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"273\" src=\"https://2.bp.blogspot.com/--Vvwy8D4ejg/T-fhU6jMsGI/AAAAAAAAMl0/9cIIuj_Qug4/s640/imagesCAMKRAUV.jpg\" width=\"640\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<br />\nThe British have post dated it to 4000 BC, considering that the big bang happened in Bible only in 4004 BC, and the fact that they have screwed it up royally by writing everywhere that the wheel was invented after 4000 BC, in Central Europe and Mesopotamia.<br />\n<br />\nWell what do they know about the wheel?<br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-thBmNeRrsf8/T-ftXEwKhEI/AAAAAAAAMnQ/UmbZaFeD-c8/s1600/mahabharata_war.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"435\" src=\"https://2.bp.blogspot.com/-thBmNeRrsf8/T-ftXEwKhEI/AAAAAAAAMnQ/UmbZaFeD-c8/s640/mahabharata_war.jpg\" width=\"640\" /></a></div>\n<br />\nSo Max Muller , Macaulay and party have given a cock and bull story that these caves were created by arrows ( missiles ) from Lav and Kush- the sons of Lord Sri Rama of Ramayan war of 4300 BC.<br />\n<br />\nCheck out the picture below. font-size: large;\">The Aztec king Atahualpa wore the same 9 feather Asura king head dress.&nbsp; Peru or Patala flourished after the Asura&nbsp;master&nbsp;architect and astronomer Maya Danava ( who wrote Surya Siddhanta ) ran away to Patala.</span><br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; Now you get the drift why National Geographic calls Kerala , the most beautiful place on this planet, right?<br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<object class=\"BLOGGER-youtube-video\" classid=\"clsid:D27CDB6E-AE6D-11cf-96B8-444553540000\" codebase=\"http://download.macromedia.com/pub/shockwave/cabs/flash/swflash.cab#version=6,0,40,0\" data-thumbnail-src=\"http://3.gvt0.com/vi/b2Q-EumWzws/0.jpg\" height=\"266\" width=\"320\"><param name=\"movie\" value=\"http://www.youtube.com/v/b2Q-EumWzws&fs=1&source=uds\" />\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n<param name=\"bgcolor\" value=\"#FFFFFF\" />\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n<param name=\"allowFullScreen\" value=\"true\" />\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n<embed width=\"320\" height=\"266\"  src=\"http://www.youtube.com/v/b2Q-EumWzws&fs=1&source=uds\" type=\"application/x-shockwave-flash\" allowfullscreen=\"true\"></embed></object></div>\n<br />\nAs per our records, Lord Rama's brother Lakshman cut of Ravana's sister Surpaneka's nose at Edakkal caves. She was a very beautiful girl , the grand daughter of Maharishi Pulastya ( sapta rishi fame ) and NOT a ugly demon .<br />\n<br />\nThe root cause of Ramayan war is due to this incident. Noting that King Ravana&nbsp;was not eager to take revenge ( for she had misbehaved with Sita, after having a crush on handsome Rama) , she took of her bangles and told him to wear it in front of all in his court.&nbsp; <br />\n<br />\n<em><span style=\"color: blue;\">Cutting off the nose ( Naak katna ) in Indian culture is known to all.&nbsp; It does NOT mean her nose was actually cut off .</span></em><br />\n<em><span style=\"color: blue;\"><br /></span></em>\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-n9JyDkYEFkA/T-ildI3JQlI/AAAAAAAAMpo/m_7EfflpXfQ/s1600/Rama-breaks-bow-of-Shiva.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"640\" src=\"https://1.bp.blogspot.com/-n9JyDkYEFkA/T-ildI3JQlI/AAAAAAAAMpo/m_7EfflpXfQ/s640/Rama-breaks-bow-of-Shiva.jpg\" width=\"464\" /></a></div>\n<br />\nAbout 1.5 hours drive from here is Thirunelli temple and Papanashini river ( actually a stream now ).<br />\n<br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"https://4.bp.blogspot.com/-QITGh5PkNus/XKX-SJKVFFI/AAAAAAABghI/ffT77oyp1GsuRVo_16590HfUzQ2XcplhACLcBGAs/s1600/ThiruQnelli-Temple-Wayanad-2.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" data-original-height=\"315\" data-original-width=\"431\" height=\"466\" src=\"https://4.bp.blogspot.com/-QITGh5PkNus/XKX-SJKVFFI/AAAAAAABghI/ffT77oyp1GsuRVo_16590HfUzQ2XcplhACLcBGAs/s640/ThiruQnelli-Temple-Wayanad-2.jpg\" width=\"640\" /></a></div>\n<br />\nAfter the Ramayana war , Lord Rama has taken a dip here to pray for the souls of all the thousands who died in battle. Rama also did the pitru karma for his father King Dasharatha here.<br />\n<br />\nThis place as holy as Banares of Ganges river&nbsp;. Lord Brahma himself has installed the idol of Vishnu here. As such it is one of the oldest idols of this planet. <br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-a2eGaHD6lus/T-fsoVabN_I/AAAAAAAAMnA/gim11iKx_rY/s1600/Papanasini.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; Vishnu's footstep is seen on a rock.</span><br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-iGc7-Fro3as/T-ft7m2DGfI/AAAAAAAAMng/J9QJH5EDsi0/s1600/Wayanad%2520Elephants%25206.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://2.bp.blogspot.com/-iGc7-Fro3as/T-ft7m2DGfI/AAAAAAAAMng/J9QJH5EDsi0/s1600/Wayanad%2520Elephants%25206.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<em><span style=\"color: blue;\">Below script at Edakkal caves is one in the eye for all those who have their own ideas about who wrote which language first -- and from where.</span></em><br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-m-Tc6X8aQX0/T-fvjVWUbWI/AAAAAAAAMn4/mdEMh0hmPDY/s1600/21.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"377\" src=\"https://4.bp.blogspot.com/-m-Tc6X8aQX0/T-fvjVWUbWI/AAAAAAAAMn4/mdEMh0hmPDY/s640/21.jpg\" width=\"640\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Bishop Robert Caldwell\n(1814\u20131891) was an Christian Evangelist missionary and linguist, who came to\nIndia to poison Hindusim, by translating and printing books in Tamil. He got\ninto a deal with Tamilian Iyers for plum administrative posts in the British\nRaj.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-_NMsNR8oIIA/UYw8pU8oQ4I/AAAAAAAAiJg/jfflNh_MAzA/s1600/150px-Robert_Caldwell.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"320\" src=\"https://4.bp.blogspot.com/-_NMsNR8oIIA/UYw8pU8oQ4I/AAAAAAAAiJg/jfflNh_MAzA/s320/150px-Robert_Caldwell.jpg\" width=\"237\" /></a></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">For poisoning the Hindu\ntexts , in return he established Tamil as the oldest language\u2014which gave an ego\nmassage to Tamils. Some of the\npadres were professional printers and&nbsp;\nlinguists in religious garb. To convert they need the Bible in local\nlanguage. The ancient Tamil heritage is so glorious. They have forgotten all\nthat, as all the old palm leaf manuscripts have been burnt by the missionaries.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">The Italian priest\nRobert de Nobili (1577-1656). d called himself a \u2018Roman Brahmin\u2019. Let me list\nout a few 3 in 1 missionaries\u2014padre/ printer/ proselytisers. Italian\nmissionary, Constantine Joseph Beschi (1680-1746), who called himself\nVeeramaamunivar (Veer-Maha-Munivar),&nbsp;\nGerman missionary Barthalomaus Ziegenbalg (1683-1719) who called himself\nZiegenbalg Iyer,&nbsp; Englishman G.U. Pope\n(1820-1907) who called himself \u201cPope Iyer.\u201d, Scotsman Robert Caldwell\n(1814-1891) who along with his wife Elissa Mault did massive conversions by\noffering sops, Portuguese missionary John De Britto etc etc. <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">The Madras Catholic\nDiocese, has been on a amazing campaign that, \u201cThiruvalluvar was a disciple of\nSt. Thomas and that Thirukkural have been lifted&nbsp; from the teachings of St. Thomas\u2014nonsense. &nbsp;How could people like Karunanidhi allow this\nif they have some pride in Tamil heritage , culture and pride<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-GMcEvbx4hLo/T-fuNSwbBEI/AAAAAAAAMno/VAP3p8W-wEk/s1600/ddd.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://4.bp.blogspot.com/-GMcEvbx4hLo/T-fuNSwbBEI/AAAAAAAAMno/VAP3p8W-wEk/s1600/ddd.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n&nbsp;CAPT AJIT VADAKAIL<br />\n..<br />\n<br /></div>\n", "author": {"id": "14410812789424637654", "displayName": "Capt. Ajit Vadakayil", "url": "https://www.blogger.com/profile/14410812789424637654", "image": {"url": "//4.bp.blogspot.com/-QSnd-Z8F7Kc/XFtPudWdwlI/AAAAAAABfq4/vxrkFOO7Iu8Mf6-OaPgw6FPpRDSmMgLdgCK4BGAYYCw/s35/capt%25252BajitC%25252Bvadakayil.JPG"}}, "replies": {"totalItems": "78", "selfLink": "https://www.googleapis.com/blogger/v3/blogs/3564735312144269387/posts/6123031301109853406/comments"}}, {"kind": "blogger#post", "id": "6736659894125283913", "blog": {"id": "3564735312144269387"}, "published": "2012-06-25T06:51:00+05:30", "updated": "2012-06-25T06:51:06+05:30", "etag": "\"iHf3yWDE_geBgZ8U7rgZ_xuTeAQ/dGltZXN0YW1wOiAxMzQwNTg3MjY2ODQzCm9mZnNldDogMTk4MDAwMDAK\"", "url": "http://ajitvadakayil.blogspot.com/2012/06/tankcleaning-procedures-on-chemical.html", "selfLink": "https://www.googleapis.com/blogger/v3/blogs/3564735312144269387/posts/6736659894125283913", "title": "TANKCLEANING PROCEDURES, ON CHEMICAL TANKERS-  CAPT AJIT VADAKAYIL", "content": "<div dir=\"ltr\" style=\"text-align: left;\" trbidi=\"on\">\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-AE8YIkMyIiI/T-e6kyp3r-I/AAAAAAAAMk4/n99vyGnHiaU/s1600/imagesCA0O0WVC.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-AE8YIkMyIiI/T-e6kyp3r-I/AAAAAAAAMk4/n99vyGnHiaU/s1600/imagesCA0O0WVC.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n</div>\n<br />\n\n\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<b style=\"mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 16pt; line-height: 150%;\">TANKCLEANING\nPROCEDURES, ON CHEMICAL TANKERS- <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>CAPT\nAJIT VADAKAYIL<o:p></o:p></span></b></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-nhJd6rvzKGM/T-e79RQL1yI/AAAAAAAAMlA/JG1CUvtAb6U/s1600/SAM_3678.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"300\" src=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-nhJd6rvzKGM/T-e79RQL1yI/AAAAAAAAMlA/JG1CUvtAb6U/s400/SAM_3678.jpg\" width=\"400\" /></a></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt; text-align: justify;\">\n<br /></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt; text-align: justify;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Tank\ncleaning is usually done with water, unless the cargo ROB in tank creates a\nstubborn residue like Isocyanates, in which case a non-reactive solvent must be\nused. Isocyantes will form stubborn Urethane and CO2 gas in large quantities\nwith water.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt; text-align: justify;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Esters\nand chlorinated HC will<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span>slowly hydrolyse\nto acids. This is allright in epoxy tanks if the tank cleaning is uninterrupted\nat the prewash stage . SS can handle the pH of the acid. <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt; text-align: justify;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">It\nis most important to know the next cargo planned to be loaded . Washing to WW\nstandard after a particular cargo is not as critical.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt; text-align: justify;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">No\ncleaning can take place unless the mandatory prewash as required by MARPOL is\ndone.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt; text-align: justify;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Substances\nwith high VP can be removed from tank by evaporation, unless they leave a\nstubborn residue or contain inhibitors.<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;\n</span>The NVM content of the chemical data sheet must be consulted. Any\ninhibitor not washed off will be difficult to remove and will have a bad\ninfluence on the next cargo or fail the WWT. Most inhibitors are fully soluble\nin water.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt; text-align: justify;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">The\nmaster must enforce precautions like \u201c no smoking \u201c and \u201c AC on recirc \u201c.<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span>It is important for all on a chemical tanker\nto know the location of AC fresh air intake, and the Anemometer , to use the\nrelative wind direction to advantage.<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;\n</span>Bioaccumulative vapours and carcinogenic fumes can enter the engine room\nvia intake vents and cause health problems for the engine staff. It is not all\nright to say that just the deck crew are exposed to toxic vapors.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt; text-align: justify;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Water\nwashing can be done even if the solubility of the chemical in water is low to\nas much as 0.3%.<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span>such solubility always\nincreases if the water temperature is higher. Hence always try to use wash\nwater at high temperature ( about 25 deg higher than MP after removing cold ballast\ninterface ) unless the cargo being cleaned does not allow it, like drying oils\nand mineral oils with high paraffin content. <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>Solidified matter when melted flows away with\nthe stripped out water, it need not be soluble. <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt; text-align: justify;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Mineral\noils with high paraffin content and certain crude oils which require heating\nduring transportation should always be cleaned with ambient wash to prevent\nevaporation of lighter fractions which would leave a waxy residue on tank\nbulkheads. <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span><o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt; text-align: justify;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Drying\noils if prewashed with hot water will polymerize. Drying oils must be washed\nimmediately after dischg with ambient water. If they are left to dry\npolymerization takes place due to reaction with oxygen, and heat increases the\nreaction speed. This means by removing the air form the tank using Nitrogen\nthis process can be slowed down. By the way, Ambient means upto 35 deg C.\nModerate means upto 60 deg. Hot means &gt;60 deg C.<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span><o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt; text-align: justify;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Certain\ncargoes like acetic acid, benzene, luboils, caustic soda, paraffin, molasses,\nphenol, DINP, fatty alcohols, HMD , Hitec, WPAC, butyl acrylate , creosote\netc<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span>can be hot pre-washed. <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt; text-align: justify;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">However\nif you hot prewash Styrene monomer or Acrylic acid polymerization will\nhappen.<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span>The hotter the water, the faster\nthe polymerization. Due to condensation of vapour , inhibitor free liquid is\nformed, as the inhibitor is not volatile. Inhibitor if not removed will affect\nthe PTT test. <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt; text-align: justify;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">When\na cargo is fully soluble in water, using tank cleaning chemicals in a mindless\nmanner does more harm than good. <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt; text-align: justify;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Cleaning\nthe tanks is just not enough. Most often it is the tank appendages which cause\nhuge cargo claims or tank rejection. PV valves, vent lines, fixed pipelines ,\nportable manifold hoses, superstrip lines, sampling and drain cocks, air/\nnitrogen/ steam portable connection stubs, pump internals , cofferdams \u2013all can\nhold contaminant matter. With certain cargoes like LSHW FO even the butterfly\nvalve Teflon seals can trap sludge and discolor the next cargo.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt; text-align: justify;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Washing\ntanks with portable/ fixed Butterworth machines from designated areas may not\nclean everything. This is why it is important to enter the tank and have a\nvisual check before wasting fresh water and expensive tank cleaning chemicals\nafter high MP cargoes like palm oil fatty acids. As soon as you open the tank\ndome you get a general idea of shadow areas. </span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt; text-align: justify;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt; text-align: justify;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">The chief officer must know if the\ntank corrugations are horizontal or vertical. Horizontal corrugations mean that\nfixed tank cleaning machines which cannot be given drops are ineffective.\nVertical corrugations mean that the position of the butterworth port is\nimportant.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt; text-align: justify;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Some\nof the butterworth heaters may not be able to deliver the correct temperature\nand pressure in cold winter. In such case use lesser tank cleaning machines to\nget more temperature with correct pressure.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt; text-align: justify;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">If\nthe previous cargo is strong smelling like Acrylates or Crude Turpentine or\nMTBE a smell killer can be used. Gaskets emit smell, hence they must be flushed\nwith methanol.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt; text-align: justify;\">\n<b style=\"mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">STAGES OF TANKCLEANING:--<o:p></o:p></span></b></div>\n<b style=\"mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;\"><i style=\"mso-bidi-font-style: normal;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"mso-list: Ignore;\">1)<span style=\"font-size-adjust: none; font-stretch: normal; font: 7pt/normal &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span></span></span></i></b><b style=\"mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;\"><i style=\"mso-bidi-font-style: normal;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Precleaning\nwith sea water.<o:p></o:p></span></i></b><br />\n\n\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoListParagraphCxSpLast\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt; mso-add-space: auto; text-align: justify;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Pre cleaning is different from\nMARPOL mandatory Prewash. Tank cleaning machines may have shadow sectors , and\nthis can be rectified for main wash. Non drying oils and fats can be steamed\nbefore the hot water precleaning. <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 3.05pt 0in 0pt; &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Tank\nCleaning Chemical wash <o:p></o:p></span></i></b><br />\n\n\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoListParagraphCxSpLast\" 150%;\">If cargo is not water soluble or\nresidues remain , the use of&nbsp; tank cleaning chemicals is justified. <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>If the previous cargo is not water soluble\nusing a 0.04% detergent wash will be good enough for WW standard ( this is not\nWALL WASH ).<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span>Graco barrel pump injecting into the tankcleaning line , is the best\nas the bottom can be kept stripped and tank cleaning chemical is not\nreused.<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span>Inject at the rate of 2 litres\nchemical per cubic text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-enQzM9rBnEc/T-NIdTnWZlI/AAAAAAAAMeQ/OLXL1_aFhZc/s1600/images+(3).jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-enQzM9rBnEc/T-NIdTnWZlI/AAAAAAAAMeQ/OLXL1_aFhZc/s1600/images+(3).jpg\" /></a></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\"></span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">During REM ( rapid movement of eyes ) sleep exchange of\ninformation takes place between the left lobe and right lobe of the brain. In 9\nhours of sleep there will be 6 such cycles. <span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 115%; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-language: AR-SA; mso-fareast-font-family: Calibri; mso-fareast-language: EN-US; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-latin;\">During REM sleep, the heart rate increases, oxygen\nconsumption is high, and neural firing is as active as it is during a period of\nwakefulness .\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">The brains capacity to\nstore information is disrupted when no REM sleep is experienced.<o:p></o:p></span></span></span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">\n\n<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-KtoW0kh_Nxs/T-NHPZrLgoI/AAAAAAAAMdA/ZESSfKlVerM/s1600/images+(1).jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-KtoW0kh_Nxs/T-NHPZrLgoI/AAAAAAAAMdA/ZESSfKlVerM/s1600/images+(1).jpg\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">TURIYA means \u201cconsciousness\nminus thinking\u201d . It represents consciousness free from material influence or supreme\nconsciousness . In Turiya there is the absolute awareness . It is the\nexperience of ultimate reality and truth.&nbsp;<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\"></span>In Turiya, the self does not think, feel, or\ndo, but rather observes thought, emotion, and action capable of truly\nunderstanding the totality of the universe. Turiya has no limits and no\nendpoint. It is infinitely transcendent, which means its potential is forever\nexpanding.&nbsp;<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-Ww_xAIkDUQU/T-NJIg34pRI/AAAAAAAAMeo/3udUqqIm4g4/s1600/images+(7).jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"320\" src=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-Ww_xAIkDUQU/T-NJIg34pRI/AAAAAAAAMeo/3udUqqIm4g4/s320/images+(7).jpg\" width=\"320\" /></a></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\"></span>You are now a unique\nindividual and you are a vital part of a larger universal life force that\ntranscends everything on earth.. </span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Reality and truth become more clearly defined,\nallowing you to perceive that which lies above, below, and beyond the human\nexperience. </span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">This utterly quiet, peaceful and blissful state is the ultimate aim\nof all spiritual activity this highest state is not affected by Maya The Waker,\nThe Dreamer, The Deep Sleeper and The Observer <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-sadoxGcQU5I/T-NHclopAqI/AAAAAAAAMdQ/TKPbWlYRqMA/s1600/DFJJ.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"299\" src=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-sadoxGcQU5I/T-NHclopAqI/AAAAAAAAMdQ/TKPbWlYRqMA/s400/DFJJ.jpg\" width=\"400\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Turiya is freedom from\nthe limitation of the other states . You experience detachment and joy . <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>Turiya Consciousness <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>is the ultimate goal of spirituality for here you\nknow what freedom is all about.&nbsp;<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\"></span>The dot,\npoint, or bindu of OM symbol represents the fourth state, the absolute\nconsciousness, which encompasses, permeates, and is the other three\u2014this is Turiya.\n(Silence after A, U, and M of OM Mantra) <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Piercing the bindu\nfinally allows one to attain the highest experience, and this comes after\nfollowing the process of Kundalini Awakening. <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>Turiya is regarded as synonymous with\nvidehamukti, liberation without a body. . </span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-zXRVGqdPENY/T-NHjENyvFI/AAAAAAAAMdY/XTBzSLRPRm4/s1600/bfss.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"299\" src=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-zXRVGqdPENY/T-NHjENyvFI/AAAAAAAAMdY/XTBzSLRPRm4/s400/bfss.jpg\" width=\"400\" /></a></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">A saint is a very ordinary guy.. A\nsage is the extraordinary being. A sage does not dream, because he has no\npolarity. He\u2019s just a witness. </span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">When you become a witness in your life, life\nbecomes absolutely simple. . You cannot call it waking, because this witness\nnever sleeps; you cannot call it dreaming, because for this witness no dream\never appears; you cannot call it sleep, because this witness never sleeps. </span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">It\nis eternal awareness, this is Nirvana or enlightenment <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><strong>OM is the four states\nof consciousness, as per Patanjali Yoga.</strong></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">OM is the <strong>waking state\nor jagrat</strong>. Beta brain wave</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">OM is the <strong>dreaming\nstate or svapna</strong>. <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>REM sleep state</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">OM is the <strong>deep sleep state or sushupti</strong>. (dream-less\ndeep sleep state , the delta brain wave)</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Om is the<strong>\ntranscendental state or turiya</strong>. (beyond all the states) , the fourth has been\ncalled nirvana.</span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Four stages:\nconsciousness plus thinking is waking, consciousness minus thinking is turiya,\nunconsciousness plus thinking is dreaming, unconsciousness minus thinking is\nsleep.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-sNIYflHssyk/T-NGmEtvrBI/AAAAAAAAMcg/1Fz7aHcbp98/s1600/TFSA.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-sNIYflHssyk/T-NGmEtvrBI/AAAAAAAAMcg/1Fz7aHcbp98/s1600/TFSA.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Finally, the semi-circle\nsymbolizes Maya and separates the dot from the other three curves. It is the\nillusion of Maya that prevents us from the realization of this highest state of\nbliss. The semi-circle is open at the top and does not touch the dot. This\nmeans that this highest state is not affected by Maya. Maya only affects the\nmanifested phenomenon.&nbsp;<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\"></span>In Turiya thoughts\nsubside and one becomes increasingly more awake; the mind settles down and\nconsciousness itself becomes primary. Mediators describe this as pure\nconsciousness or unbounded awareness. One sees the entire world and all things\nwithin it as part of oneself, and oneself part of all.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span></span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Turiya <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>is a state of transcendence, the result of\narduous meditation. <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>There can be no\nconsciousness without passage through intense pain. The Upanishads equates this\nexperience with enlightenment.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">We ordinary people lack\ncontact with our fourth state of consciousness, and so we fail to live up to\nour potential as human beings. <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-kU0gY5njeXc/T-NHrqy807I/AAAAAAAAMdg/eafxS39jSsI/s1600/SFHY.png\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"299\" src=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-kU0gY5njeXc/T-NHrqy807I/AAAAAAAAMdg/eafxS39jSsI/s400/SFHY.png\" width=\"400\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Turiya is the totality\nof everything, and the headwaters from which all consciousness flow. It is said\nin the Mandukya Upanishad. It is \u201cunseen, transcendent, the sole essence of the\nconsciousness of self, the completion of the world.\u201d </span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Yogis attempt to fully\nrealize the state of Turiya through practice, engaging in sound resonance,\nbreathing exercises, and body forms. Turiya yoga emphasizes a complete freedom,\nrejecting force and power, and instead embracing the ideal of a universal\nharmony. </span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Turiya is the Reality eternal, beyond all phenomena. Turiya is\nSatchidananda \u2014Existence, Consciousness, and Delight. </span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">It is here, that a highly\nadvanced seer or a spiritual Grand Master can actually hear the soundless\nsound, \u2018 AUM \u2019, the supreme secret of the Creator . </span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">In Turiya there is total\nmental clarity, and complete inner peace one recognizes the Self in every\nshining atom of existence The fourth state (turiya) corresponds closely to\ntheta state of brain function. <o:p></o:p></span></div>\nTuriya is beyond Samadhi. Samadhi is sleepless sleep.<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"color: red; font-size: large;\"><span style=\"background-color: yellow;\">It is not considered a\nstate in Vedic<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span>Indian texts</span>, rather it\nis an absence of states (dualistic or otherwise), and in Turiya; the\npractitioner is able to transcend into advaitya-- Into universal onene</span>ss.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-ZR6scajCmmI/T-NHx8Xsq4I/AAAAAAAAMdo/ajUNROX6hIQ/s1600/400922_253279821409665_174120649325583_564923_1915638682_n.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-ZR6scajCmmI/T-NHx8Xsq4I/AAAAAAAAMdo/ajUNROX6hIQ/s1600/400922_253279821409665_174120649325583_564923_1915638682_n.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">The ancient Vedic Maharishis\nwanted to go beyond nature and realize the transcendental nature of man. They\ndared to take up this challenge and the Upanishads are the unique record of the\nmethods they adopted, the struggles they undertook and the victory they\nachieved in this astonishing adventure of human spirit . </span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">The sages who\ndiscovered them had depersonalized themselves in the search for truth. Unlike\nmodern Western philosophers who lift ideas without any understanding and patent\nit in their names. </span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">They had the choice to utilize the leisure either to conquer\nthe pleasures outer world or the<span style=\"color: red;\"> painful passage to the inner.</span> </span><br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-9zRgl7emWE4/T-VT1ZXP9fI/AAAAAAAAMf4/WhtEb5rjo2c/s1600/SGJKK.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"207\" src=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-9zRgl7emWE4/T-VT1ZXP9fI/AAAAAAAAMf4/WhtEb5rjo2c/s320/SGJKK.jpg\" width=\"320\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">With their\nmental gifts, they had turned their mental energies to the conquest of the\ninner world rather than of the world of matter and life at the sensate level. </span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-CAYWspY_JOA/T-NIxTwlXzI/AAAAAAAAMeg/azKq9wc5QDU/s1600/EHI.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"241\" src=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-CAYWspY_JOA/T-NIxTwlXzI/AAAAAAAAMeg/azKq9wc5QDU/s320/EHI.jpg\" width=\"320\" /></a></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">In\nthe 7000 year old Upanishads we get a glimpse into the workings of the minds of\nthe great ancient Indian thinkers who were unhampered by the tyranny of\nreligious dogma of men who became brokers of Gods or Gods themselves , burnings\nat the stake, political authority, pressure of public opinion, seeking truth\nwith single-minded devotion, rare in the history of thought. </span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">These Indian sages\nwere not satisfied with their intellectual speculations. They discovered that\nthe universe remained a mystery and the mystery only deepened with the advance\nof such knowledge, and one of the important components of that deepening\nmystery is the mystery of man and consciousness. The Upanishads became aware of\nthis truth, which modern science now emphasizes. </span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-rFLP18jfeIE/T-NH4AB5skI/AAAAAAAAMdw/1TQK9ZcX35g/s1600/GTHBCX.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"394\" src=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-rFLP18jfeIE/T-NH4AB5skI/AAAAAAAAMdw/1TQK9ZcX35g/s400/GTHBCX.jpg\" width=\"400\" /></a></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">The purpose of the Vedas was\nto ensure the true welfare of all beings, worldly as well as spiritually.\nBefore such a synthesis could be achieved, there was a need to penetrate the\ninner worlds to its depth. This is what the Upanishads did with precision and\ngave us the science of the self, which helps man leave behind the body, the\nsenses, the ego and all other non-self elements, which are perishable. </span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">The\nUpanishads tell us the great saga of this discovery \u2014 of the divine in the\nheart of man. Upanishads in an attempt to unravel the mystery of the human mind\nand of consciousness. <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-WDZ6rkxT5Lk/T-NH-GmFGSI/AAAAAAAAMd4/YGsMOhbrl5E/s1600/imagesCA9JLT15.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-WDZ6rkxT5Lk/T-NH-GmFGSI/AAAAAAAAMd4/YGsMOhbrl5E/s1600/imagesCA9JLT15.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Upanishads, the\nBrihadaranyaka ( 1.3.28 ) says: This was my school morning assembly prayer--a 7000 year old, lofty &nbsp;Sanskrit chant.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Mangal&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">\u0950</span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"> </span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Mangal&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">\u0905\u0938\u0924\u094b</span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; I went to the radio room to give a\nmessage to my Radio Officer.</span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">He was listening to BBC\nradio. He said that BBC has announced that the Indian Hindu god Lord Ganesha\nstatues all over the planet has been drinking milk.<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span>Their camera crews had taken videos as had\nseveral other major media groups.</span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-rRPpx1faGOo/T-GRaYeSGQI/AAAAAAAAMYY/RAQKw2CIbRk/s1600/imagesCALWJ07A.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">I made the Radio\nofficer tune to other stations around the world and found that all were\nannouncing this as breaking news.</span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-GCioOxNXshM/T-GRgZAzQaI/AAAAAAAAMYg/fAmqnk147bI/s1600/imagesCA6UQ6WV.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"400\" src=\"https://1.bp.blogspot.com/-GCioOxNXshM/T-GRgZAzQaI/AAAAAAAAMYg/fAmqnk147bI/s400/imagesCA6UQ6WV.jpg\" width=\"326\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">The reason they gave\nwas some capillarity action, osmosis, surface tension type mysterious action.\nAt the same time they said that if this was the case, it is indeed a mystery\nthat statues of other gods of other religions or non-gods or people or\nstructures were NOT drinking milk.</span><br />\n<br />\n<span style=\"color: blue; font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><em>Statues of Ganesha whether it was of metal\nor stone of all sized were taking in milk--<span style=\"background-color: yellow;\">without spilling it on the ground, a</span><span style=\"background-color: yellow;\">nd the phenomenon stopped at noon..</span></em></span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-YQFvd_iBakk/T-GRmWM3inI/AAAAAAAAMYo/yucblP2UUFg/s1600/imagesCAIETLMM.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"278\" src=\"https://4.bp.blogspot.com/-YQFvd_iBakk/T-GRmWM3inI/AAAAAAAAMYo/yucblP2UUFg/s400/imagesCAIETLMM.jpg\" width=\"400\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">The whole of India was\nin absolute pandemonium. The stock markets had ground to a halt and the\ngovernment itself had shut down. For everybody in mass hysteria<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span>had run to buy milk and feed it to the\nnearest Lord Ganesha statue. Fresh milk was exhausted in India. BBC reported\nthat a milk store in England has sold an unprecedented 25,000 pints of milk.</span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<object class=\"BLOGGER-youtube-video\" classid=\"clsid:D27CDB6E-AE6D-11cf-96B8-444553540000\" codebase=\"http://download.macromedia.com/pub/shockwave/cabs/flash/swflash.cab#version=6,0,40,0\" data-thumbnail-src=\"http://0.gvt0.com/vi/exoCi2N2VxA/0.jpg\" height=\"266\" width=\"320\"><param name=\"movie\" value=\"http://www.youtube.com/v/exoCi2N2VxA&fs=1&source=uds\" />\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n<param name=\"bgcolor\" value=\"#FFFFFF\" />\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n<param name=\"allowFullScreen\" value=\"true\" />\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n<embed width=\"320\" height=\"266\"  src=\"http://www.youtube.com/v/exoCi2N2VxA&fs=1&source=uds\" type=\"application/x-shockwave-flash\" allowfullscreen=\"true\"></embed></object></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">The Radio officer\nwanted to know if Lord Ganesha was an elephant. I told him \"Ganesha has a\nelephant head and the body of an obese man . In India every Hindu will do a\nGanapathi Homam ( fire ritual with Mantra chants ) when he moves into a new\nhome -- rather even a rented house becomes a home only after this event. He is\nrevered as the God who removes all obstacles \".</span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">My ship then went to\nJapan, and the young Japanese agent was hanging around after I finished my\nofficial business with him. He was a shy type,and he wanted to talk to me about\nsome matter. So I made him comfortable with a beer. </span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">He told me that two years\nago he was in India for 4 months. He lost his job and his material girl friend.\nHe was deep in depression and was contemplating suicide, when his best friend\nto him to leave everything and take a flight to India. </span><br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-loOiAalFP6M/T-GR4Zcg8MI/AAAAAAAAMY4/_79EMZITRKY/s1600/imagesCAKR6G6A.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://2.bp.blogspot.com/-loOiAalFP6M/T-GR4Zcg8MI/AAAAAAAAMY4/_79EMZITRKY/s1600/imagesCAKR6G6A.jpg\" /></a></div>\n</div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">He landed up at Calcutta\nand got diarrhoea the very next day. He had his stock of tablets with him, as\nhe was warned by his friend that it would happen. He exhausted his stock of\nJapanese anti-diarrhoea tablets and then he went to a local doctor. He was ok,\nwithin an hour and never got diarrhoea after that. </span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">He then went into the\nHimalayan ashrams , and within a month he had found bliss. However he hung\naround for another three months exploring other holy spots at the source of the\nGanges, including Mount Kailash.</span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-6xdf4ze7-2M/T-GIQVy29wI/AAAAAAAAMXw/Et26Hfbk4vc/s1600/220px-13th_century_Ganesha_statue_cleaned_and_colour_adjusted.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"400\" src=\"https://2.bp.blogspot.com/-6xdf4ze7-2M/T-GIQVy29wI/AAAAAAAAMXw/Et26Hfbk4vc/s400/220px-13th_century_Ganesha_statue_cleaned_and_colour_adjusted.jpg\" width=\"242\" /></a></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">&nbsp;It was he who told me that many Japanese\nworship Lord Ganesha in secret, ever since Buddhism took over Japan. They keep\nthese metal statues in yin-yang Kangiten ( man-woman embrace ) form dipped in\noil at home. He said that there are more than 200 ancient Ganesha temples in\nJapan. </span><br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-noTJnNN26Zg/T-GSR8I66eI/AAAAAAAAMZA/H8-vNKG1cyk/s1600/imagesCAOG617Y.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"320\" src=\"https://3.bp.blogspot.com/-noTJnNN26Zg/T-GSR8I66eI/AAAAAAAAMZA/H8-vNKG1cyk/s320/imagesCAOG617Y.jpg\" width=\"251\" /></a></div>\n</div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">The young worship Ganesha for finding true love and discriminative\nknowledge , while the old do it for success in business, as a god of good\nfortune. </span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Since Osaka city and Tokyo ( Futako Tamagawa ) was near, by he wanted\nto take me to a Ganesha temples there.<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;\n</span>He was sure that in the royal Japanese palace Ganesha ( Daishoo Kangiten\nVinayaka ) is worshipped at Ganesh Chaturthi, since time immemorial.</span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">I did NOT find this\nhard to believe as in 7000 BC, when Emperor Vikramaditya rules the South\nEastern part of China, Ganesha was worshipped in Korea as well as Japan. Both\nin Ramayana ( 4300 BC )<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span>and Mahabharata\n( 4000 BC ) China is mentioned as Kosakara or land of silk worms.</span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-HRECnYgbz1w/T-GSa7SwnpI/AAAAAAAAMZI/jYNU2lVoSf0/s1600/104px-Kabul_ganesh_khingle.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"320\" src=\"https://4.bp.blogspot.com/-HRECnYgbz1w/T-GSa7SwnpI/AAAAAAAAMZI/jYNU2lVoSf0/s320/104px-Kabul_ganesh_khingle.jpg\" width=\"154\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<em><span style=\"color: red;\">Above 4000 year old Ganesha was found in Afghanistan.</span></em><br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Lord Ganesha is\nmentioned in the Rig Veda (2.23.1) written in 5000 BC, as the Lord of Mantras\nand seer among seers.&nbsp;</span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">When I shifted to my\nnew home , my wife got the Ganapathi Homam done. I remember staying overnight.\nThe pujari came couple of hours before dawn and started his homam. Ganesha is also called Vighnesha, the lord who removes obstaccles.</span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<object class=\"BLOGGER-youtube-video\" classid=\"clsid:D27CDB6E-AE6D-11cf-96B8-444553540000\" codebase=\"http://download.macromedia.com/pub/shockwave/cabs/flash/swflash.cab#version=6,0,40,0\" data-thumbnail-src=\"http://2.gvt0.com/vi/AuuojIo_OC4/0.jpg\" height=\"266\" width=\"320\"><param name=\"movie\" value=\"http://www.youtube.com/v/AuuojIo_OC4&fs=1&source=uds\" />\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n<param name=\"bgcolor\" value=\"#FFFFFF\" />\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n<param name=\"allowFullScreen\" value=\"true\" />\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n<embed width=\"320\" height=\"266\"  src=\"http://www.youtube.com/v/AuuojIo_OC4&fs=1&source=uds\" type=\"application/x-shockwave-flash\" allowfullscreen=\"true\"></embed></object></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">The havanam\nwas made in the drawing room with bricks and the house was full of smoke and\nsmell of incense . If you sit on the ground by the fire, where there is an\nin draft<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span>it is NOT so bad.</span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; To test use small\ncanister Freon for ionization units, small electric heater ( or steam generator\ncapsule ) for heat units and flashing light beam for infra red detector. When\ndemonstrating CO2 extinguisher the gas should not be released.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-pagination: none;\">\n<br /></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-pagination: none;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">SCBA\ncompressors must be overhauled annually and all filters replaced.<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span>After that an air quality test must be\nconducted for Carbon Monoxide &lt;5 ppm, Carbon di Oxide &lt;450 ppm, and oil\nmist &lt; 0.4 mg/ m3.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-pagination: none;\">\n<br /></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-pagination: none;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">In\ncase of PV fire during loading reduce rate to keep the flame just above the\nvent. Cut off/ quench the flame . Direct water to cool incendive spots and shut\noff loading. Flame screens are made with 28/ 28 guage to arrest flame.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-pagination: none;\">\n<br /></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; </span>Butane in nitrogen\u2014this\ngives a reading of 7.5%.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-pagination: none;\">\n<br /></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; Safe reserve of Heavy oil is 6 days for ocean voyages\u2014take into\naccount seasonal weather.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-pagination: none;\">\n<br /></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-pagination: none;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Number\nall flexible cargo hoses.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-pagination: none;\">\n<br /></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-pagination: none;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">There\nmust be a chart showing lubricant used displayed in the ECR/ CCR.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-pagination: none;\">\n<br /></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-pagination: none;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Soot\nblowers must not be operated in port . At sea the officer on bridge must be\ninformed.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-pagination: none;\">\n<br /></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-pagination: none;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">The\neconomizer circ pump should be run for at least 2 hours more after stopping ME\nto prevent soot fires and heat stress..<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-pagination: none;\">\n<br /></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-pagination: none;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Alkaline\nbatteries eye wash is 0.5 ml of Boriacic powder with half litre of water. When doing arc welding care must be taken not to overload\nthe ships generators due to high starting </span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">current.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; mso-pagination: none;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><strong>Electrical\nEquipment<o:p></o:p></strong></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; mso-pagination: none;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">\"Intrinsically\nsafe\" - an electrical circuit of connected apparatus and wiring in which\nno spark or thermal effect under normal operation or fault conditions is\ncapable of causing ignition of a given explosive mixture achieved by using low\npower circuits having limited voltages and currents<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-pagination: none;\">\n<br /></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-pagination: none;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">\"Flameproof\nEquipment\" - equipment within an enclosure capable of withstanding the\npressure<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span>developed during an internal\nignition of a flammable mixture such that any explosion generated products are\ncooled to below ignition temperature before reaching the surrounding atmosphere<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; mso-pagination: none;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Electrical\nequipment shall be de-energised and isolated before any maintenance is<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span>commenced.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-pagination: none;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">safe\nto do so.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-pagination: none;\">\n<br /></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;
