font-size: large;\"><b style=\"background-color: yellow;\"><br /></b></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"font-family: Times, Times New Roman, serif; font-size: large;\"><b style=\"background-color: yellow;\">When &nbsp;light leaves a star or the sun the\nemissions consist of pure electro magnetic radiation that is not diffracted or\nsplit by any scattering source.</b></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"font-family: Times, Times New Roman, serif; font-size: large;\"><b style=\"background-color: yellow;\"><br /></b></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"font-family: Times, Times New Roman, serif; font-size: large;\"><b style=\"background-color: yellow;\"><span style=\"color: red;\">You can look at the sun from high earth orbit\nand be blinded, but yet not see any visible light</span>.&nbsp;</b></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"font-family: Times, Times New Roman, serif; font-size: large;\"><b style=\"background-color: yellow;\"><br /></b></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"font-family: Times, Times New Roman, serif; font-size: large;\"><b style=\"background-color: yellow;\"><o:p></o:p>On earth what diffracts the light spectrum into visible\nlight is the ionosphere... There is no \"blue sky\" in space because\nthere's no atmosphere to scatter the sun's light, so the stars and planets are\nvisible all the time. &nbsp;</b></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"font-family: Times, Times New Roman, serif; font-size: large;\"><b style=\"background-color: yellow;\"><br /></b></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"font-family: Times, Times New Roman, serif; font-size: large;\"><b style=\"background-color: yellow;\"><span style=\"color: blue;\">You cannot see the\nsun in space</span>.</b></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"font-family: Times, Times New Roman, serif; font-size: large;\"><b style=\"background-color: yellow;\"><br /></b></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"font-family: Times, Times New Roman, serif; font-size: large;\"><b style=\"background-color: yellow;\">Light cannot be seen unless it's bouncing off objects or\nparticles. &nbsp; &nbsp;If matter was\ntheoretically cancelled out or hidden and you looked at a star in space with no\nmatter in between-the light would be invisible to your eyes..</b></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"font-family: Times, Times New Roman, serif;\"><o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: Times, Times New Roman, serif;\"><a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-WDY3ZEOKGjw/VcryZBwoSAI/AAAAAAAA7ww/d1fnZAB8-Fo/s1600/downloead.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"401\" src=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-WDY3ZEOKGjw/VcryZBwoSAI/AAAAAAAA7ww/d1fnZAB8-Fo/s640/downloead.jpg\" width=\"640\" /></a></span></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: Times, Times New Roman, serif;\"><br /><o:p></o:p></span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"font-family: Times, Times New Roman, serif;\"><o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: Times, Times New Roman, serif;\"><br /></span>\n<span style=\"font-family: Times, Times New Roman, serif;\">The shadows played tricks . The moon has no atmosphere. So far away hills appear closer, as the atmospheric laws don't work here.&nbsp; The uneven heights of the ground make some shadows longer. They should NOT have used wide angle lenses. The suits of the astronauts reflected the sun's light, as if they were separate light sources.</span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: Times, Times New Roman, serif;\"><br /></span>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-cq1sbBGJDtc/T98VKKvBoyI/AAAAAAAAMVg/0mLXzbISGeA/s1600/a.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, Times New Roman, serif;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"239\" src=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-cq1sbBGJDtc/T98VKKvBoyI/AAAAAAAAMVg/0mLXzbISGeA/s320/a.jpg\" width=\"320\" /></span></a></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: Times, Times New Roman, serif;\"><br /></span>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n</div>\n<span style=\"font-family: Times, Times New Roman, serif;\"><br /></span>\n<span style=\"font-family: Times, Times New Roman, serif;\">A&nbsp;lot is made of the journey through the deadly Van Allen radiation belts. &nbsp;You have to look at it in a relative manner-like a fire walker walking on hot glowing coals. The time of transit at 25000 miles an hour speed is hardly anything. The space craft was protected by aluminium and the trajectory was suitable for this exposure. In any case 94% of the surviving astronauts now suffer from cataract. </span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: Times, Times New Roman, serif;\"><br /></span>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-ej4e3okzsNs/T98V3rhTMWI/AAAAAAAAMV4/P8LLa9Mw_Mg/s1600/imagesCA0QMDBC.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, Times New Roman, serif;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"222\" src=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-ej4e3okzsNs/T98V3rhTMWI/AAAAAAAAMV4/P8LLa9Mw_Mg/s320/imagesCA0QMDBC.jpg\" width=\"320\" /></span></a></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: Times, Times New Roman, serif;\"><br /></span>\n<span style=\"font-family: Times, Times New Roman, serif;\">When weapon manufacturers boast about bullets piercing steel armour--it is at RIGHT angles. When I was putting steel plates on my ship's bridge wings, my chief engineer who had handled AK47s &nbsp;and the British guards told me that the thickness of the steel plates in NOT enough. I just told them off \" On&nbsp;my ship-- this much is enough \".</span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: Times, Times New Roman, serif;\"><br /></span>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-q6Hw2Fb7KIk/T98VTKNGrbI/AAAAAAAAMVo/kJggr18XgmQ/s1600/d.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, Times New Roman, serif;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"233\" src=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-q6Hw2Fb7KIk/T98VTKNGrbI/AAAAAAAAMVo/kJggr18XgmQ/s320/d.jpg\" width=\"320\" /></span></a></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: Times, Times New Roman, serif;\"><br /></span>\n<span style=\"font-family: Times, Times New Roman, serif;\">Then the hoax criers said, the film in the cameras should have melted. When that is NOT the way the laws of thermodynamics works in vacuum. Here heat travels by radiation--and as long as your camera is coated and the film is NOT exposed to direct rays, there is NO problem. </span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: Times, Times New Roman, serif;\"><br /></span>\n<span style=\"font-family: Times, Times New Roman, serif;\">You guys must have seen Red Adiar using mirrored shields to protect themselves from oil rig fire heat. You just need to duck behind the mirror--there is NO need for&nbsp;a fire suit.</span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: Times, Times New Roman, serif;\"><br /></span>\n<span style=\"font-family: Times, Times New Roman, serif;\">One moon day lasts as much as 15 earth days. before things got too hot the astronauts had vamoosed after collecting their rocks. Their space suits had cooling mechanisms.</span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: Times, Times New Roman, serif;\"><br /></span>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-WCungZK0ld8/T98VayfxtJI/AAAAAAAAMVw/I6WyW8HQevs/s1600/e.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, Times New Roman, serif;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"400\" src=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-WCungZK0ld8/T98VayfxtJI/AAAAAAAAMVw/I6WyW8HQevs/s400/e.jpg\" width=\"298\" /></span></a></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: Times, Times New Roman, serif;\"><br /></span>\n<span style=\"font-family: Times, Times New Roman, serif;\">Then a lot is made out of the US flag fluttering. Well you take out a folded and rolled flag, and put it on a reverse L shaped rod,&nbsp; the initial movements of the fabric with NOT follow the laws of vacuum.</span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: Times, Times New Roman, serif;\"><br /></span>\n<span style=\"font-family: Times, Times New Roman, serif;\">During APOLLO 15 mission astronaut David Scott dropped a feather and a hammer at the same time, to show that he is standing in vacuum.</span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: Times, Times New Roman, serif;\"><br /></span>\n<span style=\"font-family: Times, Times New Roman, serif;\">Now regarding no footprint being laid by the space crafts massive leg-- or lack of dust&nbsp;on the craft feet . The surface moons dust was blown off by the rocket thruster. What is below is hard and tough. </span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: Times, Times New Roman, serif;\"><br /></span>\n<span style=\"font-family: Times, Times New Roman, serif;\">Elsewhere the boots of the astronauts left marks--and they should remain for centuries as there is NO wind or air there. </span><br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-CcX0QUv3DUU/T98UBtzzlcI/AAAAAAAAMUw/_XWBrqFqXWs/s1600/g.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, Times New Roman, serif;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"400\" src=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-CcX0QUv3DUU/T98UBtzzlcI/AAAAAAAAMUw/_XWBrqFqXWs/s400/g.jpg\" width=\"398\" /></span></a></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n</div>\n<span style=\"font-family: Times, Times New Roman, serif;\"><br /></span>\n<span style=\"font-family: Times, Times New Roman, serif;\">That is why you can see so many craters. If the wind the surface would have been smooth.</span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: Times, Times New Roman, serif;\"><br /></span>\n<span style=\"font-family: Times, Times New Roman, serif;\">The rocks brought back by USA was given to many nations. I myself saw a rock piece at Calicut, my hometown. We were taken by our school,and we stood in a line with gaping mouths. These rocks are were congruent with the Soviet rock samples, scooped off by unmanned crafts.</span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: Times, Times New Roman, serif;\"><br /></span>\n<span style=\"font-family: Times, Times New Roman, serif;\">It is NO wonder that a furious Buzz Aldrin punched one of the hoax Bart Sibrel criers on his face.
